*CATEGORY AW_APCH

; Use 4 letter airport to define procedure here
; Use 3 or 4 in route for airport at end of procedure only
; If airport is used earlier in procedure, need 4 letter in route defintion
; 3 letter airport probably won't work here
; Logic handles Star and Apch in a similar manner -- don't use the same name in both categories

; May not want airport/VOR as first fix -- AI might go there instead of later point on approach,
; and AI will create 5 mile base leg from that point for some inbound directions.
; AW_STAR will not trigger direct to approach fix.  Star intended for landing in a Tracon,
; and Apch intended for landing in an active (Center) sector.

; Radius to Fix, IFP Info Gateway Search IFP Doc (NDBR)
; https://www.faa.gov/air_traffic/flight_info/aeronav/procedures
